申報無線電周刊怎樣獲得高眞實度  明　　以前無綫電廠商，製造收音機，最一注意的怎樣能使音量宏大，分隔淸楚，百强力放大管以及超外差綫路相繼採用以來，關於上述靈敏度和選擇性的問題，已毋庸多慮，可是人類的慾望是無止境的，一般工程師，又轉移其腦筋，向另一方面謀改進，最近歐美製造無綫電收音機，最著重研討的問題，便是怎樣獲得高眞實度（High　Fidelity），所謂高眞實度的意義，卽成音週率部份須能將所有各高低不同的音調，盡平衡放大之職，過去收音機因受零件的限制，大約低至40週率以下及高至5000週率以上的音調，卽不能得完全輸出，其結果自易發生失眞，尖叫，重濁聲，種種彝病。時至今日，非高眞實度的收音機，已决不能再受人歡迎。　　要獲得高眞實皮，最通用的方法，是音調控制，採用等衡器Equalizers，特殊設計變壓器，改進機件的組合。　　音調控制過去的收音機，其成音週率放大級，很顯著的缺少低過率範圍，緣於不能得有良好的成音週率變壓器及其他附件，在此種情形下，如有高週率範圍的音號，容其完全輸出，勢必發生不自然的尖叫。補救方法，可採用如圖一A所示，高週率之一部份，得自C1濾去。此高週率音調控制器用之於電阻交連級，尤為有效，若在變壓器交速級內，或將引起重濁混亂聲，又因C1連接，使變壓器調整至一固定週率，砍在此點更易發生副波的失眞。　　設或有時需使一部份的低週率音調除去，而不致引起副波，最簡單綫路如圖一B。　　以上兩種高低濾波器，亦可同時並用，使音響曲綫更形平直，完成高眞實度。　　等衡器獲得完全的高眞實度，不僅使音響曲綫平直，更須擴展其週率範圍，低至40週，高至5000週，因此種週率，實際上播音室內會時常遇到的，完成這點，最簡單方法如圖二，係一包含電容器，電阻，感應圈三者的調整綫路，此綫路記合適宜，可使所有在4005000週範圍內的音號，减低其放大力，這樣，無異的使400週以下及5000週以上的音號，自動增高其音響。　　圖二A說明普通收音機之週率與音響關係，注意在商抵週率兩溫處，曲綫垂落。圖二B表示電阻，電容器，感應圈串聯綫路之總阻與週率關係，注意週率高低兩端的總阻較中部為高，所以如以B的串聯綫路接在成音週率管的柵極回路內，如圖二C所示，自可補救牠的缺點，使兩端的音響增强，曲綫成平直，也就是獲得高眞實度。　　以上所述的等衡器，稱之為串聯等衡器。為今之最有成效者。此外另有一種常用的並聯等衡器，亦可產生高眞實度音響曲綫，如圖三，係利用吸收原理，最適宜與成音週率變壓器合用，可使一部份成音週率成短路，這樣，其情形自與上述的串聯等衡器相同。七二零英里—超短波射程的新記錄  泡　　超短波的射程，一向以為不出在高處目力所及的範圍內，用數目講，大槪是一百餘英里。但是最近，這射程竟擴張到七百二十英里！　　超短波的射程能打破一百餘里的老紀錄的，事實上已有不少例子可舉，現在為節省篇輻起見，只舉一例，美國紐約W2AMJ超短波電臺，在今年六月二十三日「東部標準鐘點」上午十一時半，被芝加哥W9KQW電台所收到，所用的波長是五公尺。　　有了這樣的新發現，過去各種解釋超短波射程的學說，當然受到影響，所以就有不少新的意見，來解釋這種新的事實。下面就是幾種新的解釋：　　甲　超短波穿過高空的電離層，受到月球或其他天體的反射，再折回地球而被收受，如第一圖。　　乙　超短波在高空受　離層的曲折及反射作用，折回地面而被收受，如第二圖。　　丙　超短波在高空，受離化程度極高的離子層的反射。而折回地面，如第三圖。　　丁　因太陽黑斑的活動，而造成超短波遠程通訊，但這說，興事實不甚和合。　　戊　一種地波說。　　己　因為海氏層的特別升高，故射程亦遠，如第四圖。　　庚　因反射層特別低，故反射後的電波尙能回到地面，如第五圖，A線因反射層太高，故反射後越過地面，B線因在較低處反射，故仍回至地面。　　本文成後，見八月份OST無線電維誌上又載一超短波射程新紀錄。此次射程超出九百英里，造成此紀錄者為W1BJ　及W8YE　二電台，當時雙方互相收發約十五分鐘，電訊强度R1至R7，時間為美國東部標準時刻午後二時一刻無綫電拾零  子泰　　（一）全波整沭管的代替物　　普通的全波整流管如遇到意外的時候，可以暫時用二隻燈絲電壓相當的三極管連接起來代替。如八十號整流管就可用二隻　A·接法如上圖。接到的PPFF四極，可以焊接在一隻舊的眞空管底部，再挿在原來八十號的眞空管座中，那末一切工作就和原來一般的進行了。　　（二）電碼練習機取用直接電源的簡單接法　　電碼練習機假使要用直接電源，可如上圖的接法。這電碼練習機旣不需用任何電池或眞空管，而用電又非常經濟。要注意的地方，就是〇一MFD的固定電容器必需雲母絕緣，而又能耐高壓電流。至於低週率變壓器可利用舊收音機中的，三比一或五比一都可以。照上述的綫路，自己做的電鍵也可以得到很良好的成績了。　　（三）揚聲器昔調的調節法　　電池式收音機的磁石揚聲器有時會發出嘈雜的細小的雜聲來，音調也就因此不十分悅耳。這補救的方法，可用固定電容器跨接在揚聲器二端，電容器的容量可自·〇〇六至·一MFD·用不同容量的電容器就可聽到不同的音調·照上圓的接法，我們就可以隨意所欲的調節揚聲器發的音調了。富星義記無綫電行修理忙　　上海福州路五二三號富星義記無綫電料行修理部對於顧客有收音機修理者莫不認眞工作儀器精密交件迅速取費低廉更有充分之保證故顧客均極滿意是以營業蒸蒸日上工作人員忙碌殊甚該行不敢自滿更努力向前茲由美國定購之最新式儀器已經運到更加聘經驗豈富之修理專門人材以實現擴大計劃俾達服務社會之眞忱誠為裝置收音機之福音也內外消息　　天目無綫電行開設於靜安寺路七五四號電話三六二六二自成立迄今營業異常發達已修過之機件顧客無不稱心滿意蓋價廉物美人皆歡迎故也該公司茲以答謝顧客使服務更能週到起見定有三大目標實行非使顧客滿意不可之計割計第一務須約期不誤以示信守第二修理不論時間祇要機件樣樣都好第三價格不計多少定使顧客滿意而後已云云。出版界出版業衰頹之檢討  器重　　在數年之前，書業鼎盛，新書店像是雨後春筍，在上海開設了不少。可是，轉賬之間，倒閉的倒閉，出盤的出盤，不倒閉而不出盤的也大都在裁員减薪，似乎有些殘喘苟延不下去的樣子。據說，這是為了整個社會經濟衰頹的綠故，大的公司銀行尙且在倒閉，書業受到影響，自然在情理之中，。然而，我們在出版業的本身上檢討一下，我們覺得社會經濟之衰頹果眞是一個很大的原因，而其本身之不健全，實為更大的原因。因為，整個的社會經濟雖然衰頹，學校裏出來的學生找不到出路，大家嚷着「畢業即失業，讀了書沒有飯吃，」但同時又現出了一個矛盾的狀態，就是每個學校的招生，投考的終要超出應取的學額，書店出版的雜誌，五六年前像商務的「東方」「敎育」「婦女」「學生」等，一直可以伸出大姆指認為銷路最大的，但不過僅是幾千份；現在開明的「中學生，北新的「新學生」，申報館的「申報月刋」，那一種不是銷路在萬數以上？即使認為銷路不佳的，至少也有二三千份，可見得書店的主顧實在比從前多得多，而書店竟會因社會經濟的關係而陷入不景氣的苦阱裏，設非其自身之不健全，終也不至於到這一個地步，這是很明白的了。所以，在目前，要使衰頹的出版事業從新復盛起來，其本身不健全的地方不能不檢討出來。　　第一點就是投機，取巧，貪圖近利，比方如民八亞東書局出了標點舊書，賺了一筆錢，於是各書店競相效法，想來分潤一些，而自己並不想一下這路是否可通，貿然為之，弄到後來資本完全擱死，無可奈何，只好一折七五扣或是一元三斤半來賠本的出淸存貨。五六年之前，馬克斯派的學說，在社會上很出風頭，於是書店老關，看到目前有利可圖，競相爭印，大有不帶左傾色彩的够不上印行的趨勢，想不到風頭一轉，老闆只好望了堆在棧房中的銷售不掉的存書而歎氣。此外，如競出兒童讀物，印行畫報，見到「論語」以幽默之態度而得到很多的讀者，於是也來照樣投機，老　們卻沒有想到跟了人家跑，前面路上的黃金早巳被前面的人拾去，自己不會拾得到什麼了。還有，看到敎科書有利可圖，自己也來印行，只求投機謀利，不問內容是否精審，更為貪圖銷售，拚命給予書賈厚利，折扣打得很大。像最近，又是競印古書，商務中華因為資本大，當然不會生問題，其他書店，也來競印，彷彿目前的出版界只有翻印古書一倏路可走，拚命的向前追去，待到跌在苦阱之中，那時就要後悔無及。所以，目前的出版界，須得自己放準眼光，望定了目標前進，不要看到人家怎樣，自己為圖目前的近利而投機而跟洛怎樣。須知盲目的跟人前進，前面的利益只有被人家得去，自己即使不隨之而失敗，但得利也很有限，這是出版界應該覺悟的。　　第二是不審書籍內容，只費名家名字。很多的書店老闆，如果碰到一個無名作家的稿子，他並不審察一下內容怎樣，以為無名作家的稿子，决不能帮他賺錢，大有稿子送給他都不要之趨勢。反過來，有名作家的稿子，不問其內喀，每肯出巨價收買。其實，無名作家的稿子，未必都是不行的，而名家的作品，雜亂無章者也多得很。讀者並不個個是有名作家之崇拜者，出了巨價去買得了名作家過時的作品或是無聊的作品，化去資本印行，銷售不掉，也只好望了大堆存書歎氣。所以，書店老翳，今後也得改變方針，出版一本書，不要在作家的名字上打算盤，最要緊的還是姿審察一本書籍的內容。　　第三是鋪張表面外强中乾。有許多書店，當其開設在弄堂裏的時候，因為開支不大，獲利很多，但是，想獲更多之利，所以把組織立刻擴大起來。那裏知道，組織擴大了，開支浩繁，而營業也不過和在弄堂裏時差不多。看看危險，想要收縮而不可能，每有因之而關鬥者。如前年×書局，將大批資本向外國去訂購最新式的印書機器，有人告以且慢實行，而老闆不聽，終於，外國的機器還沒有到上海，自己先陷於不能維持的地步。當時設非再加入資本，則外國訂購之機器來了，自己也不能使用，勢必廉價拍賣。所以，書店老闆，作事把穩，踏實了地，不要妄事鋪張，空做塲面，則不景氣的巨浪打將過來，終也不會成為致命之傷。　　第四是僅求銷廣放賬難收。因為鑑於開支浩大，於是只求銷路廣大，對於外地書賈，冀其多銷書籍，故予以巨大折扣，還將賬目拖放。那裏知道放賬容易收賬為籬，到期收得之賬目，七折八折已是幸運，而書買將大批書籍退下抵賬，書籍在途中裝來裝去，受到損失極大，放着廉價部中出售，不過聊以略略收回資本而巳。然而，書店老闆，在此已經吃假不小！不幸書籍汚損，而七折八扣之賬目又未能收得一文，使自己陷於絕地者，在現在的出版界這是常有的事。所以出版商人，應當覺悟，寗可腳踏實地，不妨營業少做，則雖然社會經濟衰頹，自己所受影響，决不至於陷於絕地。　　第五濫登廣吿徒耗金錢。廣吿不是不要登，出版界出了一本書籍，不登廣吿，人家怎麼會知道而來購買！但刋登廣吿，也得對於自己的資本算算。大的書店，資本動輒千萬或是幾百萬，他們的營業也做得很大，所以每月花上幾千元或是萬元的廣吿費，决不會感受什麼影響的。普通書店，資本不過數萬或數千，　　也遠不及大書店之廣吿，每見大書店在報紙　刊大幅廣吿，於是相率效尤，想借廣吿之力，發展自己的營業，殊不知一大幅廣吿之刊費，即耗去一書之本利數十倍。即白送去數十本書，還不能收回一天之廣告費。所以廣吿要做得醒目而又不佔多大地位，仍有效力，而每月可以節省不沙之開支，這也是出版業不景氣之狂潮中書店老闆應加以注意的。　　上述五點，據我看來是出版業頹衰而在本身上檢討出來的弱點。或者尙有其他，為我所見不到的。整理淸詞之商榷  唐養之　　淸儒焦循曰：「一代有一代之所勝，欲自楚騷以下，讓為一集，漢則專取其賦，魏晋六朝至隋，則專錄其五言詩，唐則專錄其詩，宋專錄其詞，元專錄其曲。」（易餘簽錄）余謂若淸人所勝，除說經足以越唐宋，與兩漢經生爭衡，文學固莫尙乎詞！詩有有王士正沈　潛之為唐，同光派之為宋，王關遝鄧輔綸之為漢魏六朝，然胥不能越唐宋漢魏六朝之範圍，駢散文亦然，詞則能開宋元人未有之境者也！張爾田氏疆村遺書序：以一陽淡萬氏（澍）之訂律，為詞學之一盛，吳縣戈氏（載）之審音為再盛，陽湖張氏（惠言）之尊體為二盛，而臨桂王氏（鵬連）與朱氏之校勘，為詞學之極盛。」一洵不誣也。葉恭綽氏等近纂淸詞鈔寖成，可謂淸詞一大結集矣，其餘諸家理董之者，當亦不少，爰將千慮之得，草為此篇，以供聲家之垂敎焉。　　宋人詞集，如辛棄疾王沂孫諸家，其可與南渡史實，參證不少，而鳳林書阮元草堂詩餘三卷，尤足見異族入主中原，國人排外之心理，詞之有史，由來舊矣。淸初屈大均錢謙益等詩集，列為禁書，非直以其懷故國，抑且有種族思想焉；紀宮禁秘聞焉；（謙益雖貳臣，然其於薙髮國語二事，指斥頗多。）詩旣有之，詞亦宜然，三藩之禍，海疆之變，以及入關之初，掖庭秘事，有載筆之士所不能及者，豈無意內言外之作，惜乎當時文網之嚴，或且湮沒失傳，傳者又無人為紀本事，徒令後人彷彿想象得之。若洪楊之際，蔣春霖水雲樓詞，譚獻以為「咸豐兵事，天挺此才，為倚聲家杜老。」（篋中詞識語）逮至光緒庚子之禍，王鵬運朱孝臧二家集中，尤多感事之作，此皆計時不逾百年，十口相傳，放老猶在，若不亟為爬梳箋釋，恐後亦終成疑案耳，劉知幾史通曰：「秦人不死，識符生之厚誣：蜀老猶存，知葛亮之多枉；」官書例為尊者諱，詞婉而隱，最可託諷，尤足補紀載之缺矣，（若半塘鷓鴣天詠史諸作，疆村以銜杯哀山陰王黼臣郞中，其本事詳見李岳瑞春冰室野乘。）是曰存史，一也。　　譚獻氏曰：「阮亭，　葆一流，為才人之詞；宛鄰，止庵一派，為學人之詞：惟納蘭性德，項鴻祚，蔣春霖三家，是詞人之詞；」而自來論淸詞者，亦有浙派常州派之別，近代若玉錫振，蘇謙，陳灃，葉衍蘭，王鵬運，况　顧諸家，情粵要西人也，亦可謂之粵派，然終平若譚氏之說為妥，（若譚氏及朱孝臧，皆浙人也，而趨向乃在常州派）况淸代詞家輩出，玉石雜糅，音之選淸詞者，若王昶氏之國朝（原題不便追改）詞綜四十八卷，黃燮淸氏之國朝詞綜績編二十四卷，尠有論及，况在中葉以前，驗亦不能窮其變，譚氏　中詞，雖觸類引伸，往往有中肯綮之語，然其書續集以下，旋得旋鈔，實無系統。今宜仿馮煦宋六十一家詞選之例，人係以論，　而為周濟宋四家詞選，取開山各派　人為之冠，亦不限於四家，而餘子相近者附見焉，是曰別派，二也。　　宋元人詞，見於永樂大典諸家筆記等書，今人頗從事於輯佚工作，然亡失已不知其幾，因宋元人不能錄而存之也。淸代不以詞名家，而名篇隱秀，不容湮沒者，或散見於雜著等書，此等書於後世傳不傳未可知，在六藝諸子，著錄於漢書藝文志者，至惰響經籍志，已非其舊，即無水火之劫，兵戎之禍，已在可慮，與其使後之人，於故紙堆中，窺其一鱗半爪，母寗今日即為此工作，互為一集，是曰搜逸，三也。　　清代別集之多，汗牛充棟，猶不足以為形容調，可傳者實不及什一，而名家或轉為所挨，若董晋卿氏齊物論齋詞，譚獻選篋中詞至於寤寐求之不能得，僅於選本中輯存二闋。吾鄉（松江）姚春木氏名椿，丁詩古文辭，傳桐城之學，輯有國朝文錄及所著通藝閣詩文集，皆行世，又有灑雪詞，長調能異軍突起，而後嗣式微，迄今無人為之刋行。吾以為與其將自己百無聊賴之作品，被人拉雜摧燒，毋寗流播先賢名著乎？是曰表微，四也。　　綜上諸說：第一點雖亦有人從事，而不能成為專書。第二點自非專家，不能為役。第三點則鮮有及之矣。第四點淸代及今人已有為之者，誠能得大有力者，彙為專門叢書，其功當不在毛晉等下矣。　　周濟氏宋四家詞選　論曰：「由衷之誠，豈不或亮，其或不亮，然余誠矣。」愚誣之見，竊以援斯例也。中國農村經濟資料  菱湖昭　　馮和法編　黎明書局出版　　因為中國的農村經濟破產，於是引起許多專家對於中國經濟問題的研究與論爭。近幾年來，中國社會史的論戰，可謂盛極一時，推其原因，只不過是嚴重的實際需要所反映出來。　　至於中國社會史的論戰，其最後目標，係在乎解决中國農村的經濟問題。對這問題的討論，各專家以立塲不同，當然各有各的特殊的觀察，而得到相異的結果。我們在各雜誌報章上的論文，各家發揮中國農村經濟各方面，似乎都缺乏實際的資料作本問題的理論根據，於是，就犯了這個「論據不確」的毛病。　　這一本「中國農村經濟資料，」著者委實耗費許多時間和精神來搜集各項調查資料。據著的搜集，除那過去各處舉行之實地查考分縣分村外，只單就挨戶調查，從一九二七年到現在已有數十次之多，若將分縣分村等包含在內，恐有百外次呢。不過那些調查和報吿，不是零零星星的統計，便是易糢糊的油印紙張，因此各家拿來引用，每多顧此失彼，仍有「論據不實」之病，可不是嗎？　　這本「中國農村經濟資料，」便是最近過去各種報吿及專論的搜集。較其他專家編著的中國農村經濟調查或報吿，勝過許多，凡一切主要的已都包括在本書內了。　　本書的「唯一」長處，便是搜集的豐富和詳細。不論是中國農村的複雜情形，抑或是農村經濟破產的狀况，在本書裏可以顯然地看出來。並且還有一點便利地方，本書各項資料，完全按着年代的演進，瞧起來更是便當許多。讀後，對於中國農村經濟的崩潰原因，至少可以得到一個綜合的概念。進而研究或從事於農村複興和農村建設，無疑可得到很多的有力的參考。

申報本埠增刊談言意阿事件之預測  吹　　據前日報載，國聯特委會建議案已送出，意大利斷難接受，意代表阿洛錫曾，因賴伐爾之力勸，將返意親懇莫索里尼接受云云，該建議案雖未公表其全部，但就「明白規定不得有類似意國對阿之軍事，或政治統治，聞並應宣佈阿國準備接受外國之助力，而使發展及警備其土地，」一項言之，早知意國之决雞接受矣。　　但土耳其代表對於五國委員會所草擬建議案，認為對於阿國，太不公道，蘇聯外長李維諾夫，將於明日在行政院中，抨擊此種方案，預料一般小國，皆將追隨李維諾夫，對五國委員會之調解方案，提出抗議，卽趨上兩說觀之，在一方面現未能滿足意國的慾望，而在另一方面，則尙未滙一般公道之人心也。　　意首相莫索里尼，自建設法西斯主義的國家之後，整軍經武，當欲一顯其好身手，於是借了兩個題目，一個在過去的四十年的舊事，意國右阿國吃過了一個敗仗，現在欲來雪以前的恥，一個在凡爾賽和約成功以後，意國沒有得到相當的殖民地，現在欲來算篇舊賬，這原是一舉兩得的事。　　不料阿圖不甘屈服，偏要和意國較量一下，拼個你死我活，天然意國燕甘示弱，非以武力征服他們不可，其實阿國之所以敢如此強硬，自然有後臺勞闆撑腰，不過起初還不好露面，及至迭次調解無成，不得不顯露出自已的面目，因此意阿的衝突，將一變為意英的衝突了。　　但試揭開地圖一看，地中海，和紅海，蘇彝士河，盡屬英國的海軍根據地，而菲洲的地方，又為英人勢力範圍，故阿比西尼亞的國家，差不多是英國的禁止，怎肯被意國獨自併吞，此種情形，擺在眼前，不消推測而知，故意國人有句幽默的語曰，英國可以對於日德，非常懦弱，而對於素來友好的意國，何强硬乃爾，此語已將英國的心事，完全道破。　　假定此次英意而果然開開，勝負之數，究將誰屬，雖難預料，但以以聯的情形，和地勢上的關係，勝利之數，屬於英國的多，因為英國旣有龐大的海軍

Page 20

力，而地中海又為英人的勢力圈，並且此次意國對阿用兵，名義上似不大正當，所以難得各國的同情，現在已有十數國軍艦，雲集地中海，待命國聯對意發動，則英國非特海軍勢力，優於意國，亦得人助者多也。　　不過新興的德國，要求軍備平等，未達目的以後，卽退出國聯，現在正不聲不響，埋頭苦幹，待時而動，最近希特勒向國會宣言，酷愛和平，矢志不渝，整軍目的，在保衛本身自由，不欲干涉他人的事，惟念念不忘米美爾並與共產黨為死敵云，其言雖如此，萬一不忘凡爾賽的恥辱，借英意的戰事，來恢復自己的立塲，而與意國合作，則英意勝負之數，未可知矣。　　至其時所難决定者，便是俄美的態度問題，該兩國的加入戰團，有舉足重輕的趨勢，但世界至此，已呈不堪設想，故莫索里尼，此次能接特委會的建議案，息事寗人，至為大幸，否則恐怖的局面，眞有非我人所能想像得到者。　　按前日報載，曾有意代表阿洛錫，應賴伐爾之要求，將返意力勸墨相之說，據昨日報載，則旣經墨相拒絕，阿氏亦應不返意矣，果如此則意阿形勢愈加險惡，並聞德意又有互相諒解之說，則歐局形勢何堪設想耶。秋天閑話  華木　　對於季節的替換，我從來都似乎缺少一點銳感。樹木未經敷成翠綠，花草未經放出燦爛之前，我總覺得春天離開人間還很遼遠；夏天除太陽炙熱一些叫人難受之外，我也分不出它會比春天可厭，所謂春天己經完塲了。至以看見滿地落紅，大發其傷春惜春的感慨，心里從來可也不曾有過這樣鄭重的想作。看來，心腸雖難免說過於頑硬，其實在我覺得倒很恬然自在。彷彿有人說過，情感易動的人卽非福相。生當離亂之世，縱想韜光養晦都不可能；在連串壓來的苦怕人事之中，少此一塲「少年心事，」也未始不是「幸福」的。因為我覺得這是多少在保存着自已的「眞」態。　　許多騷人墨客的詩文里，傷春悲秋就是他們大好的材料，說來有聲有色。其中雖然也還分成兩種姿態，一是裘馬詩人的濫調，一是淸定文士的感嘆，在藝術的沽價上不能混為一談的。不過我之恬然自得於自己的不會傷春悲秋，也决不是有什麼譏諷他人的意思。也許就是平庸的日子，一季一季的將生命打發下去，雖非裘馬中人。也還不至飢寒末路，就因此覺得兩邊都無自己挿足餘地，而於季節的替換也就漠然；與文章一事更少關係了。自然，許多密士們的傷春感秋之作也能叫我非常感動。但這究竟是他人的事，他人的文。讀前與讀後的情戚就有很遠的差距的。九月衣裳未剪裁，全家都在秋風里。這樣的句子也只有貧寒的黃仲則纔寫得出，寫來也恰合身份。日子稍為過得好的人，那是不會覺到秋風有這樣可怕的威力的。　　算來，　天早就結束了的，過得兩天又是萬家兒女拜月華的中秋了。所謂秋天實已過了一半。直到現在纔來寫這篇關於秋令的小文，自己想來都覺過鈍得可笑，也許就帶有不少無聊的臭味。但這也只能怪自己天生的鈍戚，無法補救。談到中秋，自己作客他鄉，已無親族，復鮮高貴友朋，縱屬佳節，實際都與自己無甚關係，要嘗嘗月餅的滋味，也只有自己去買來吃。至謂賞月那又極其平淡的。從冬而春而夏直到現在，在我的容前就經看了賞了不知幾回次的由圓而缺，由缺而圓的月色，這樣的日子久了，月與我幾乎已打成一體，實在想不出賞月之類的韻事還有什麼樂趣。然而這决不是我的性情本來怪耿若此，作事時我雖需要有個安靜地方，消遣時可還是醉心熱閙；獨行獨往到底會叫我寂寞難耐。也許是一個人的生活條件還未臻裕餘的時候，就很難溶浹於世俗趣味里。　　可是，秋天到底已過了一半了。黃昏午夜，梧桐樹梢的風聲繁露，確帶來不少蕭瑟的冷意，以後的日子當會日漸蕭條下去，黃葉西風，霜林萎草，也將在轉瞬之間卽把大地裝成一副嚴肅凄凉的面孔，再下去，就是比秋天試來得凄凉蕭索，嚴肅冰冷的冬天了。這樣的日子當然不會使我高興。自己尙未到達中年，自無從了解，體味到中年人的心境。也許中年人對於秋天情感就易於流於悲楚，所謂因景致，情觸了與己年齡的切膚痛癢關係。人生數十寒暑耳，一到中年，生命力正走到蓬勃與萎縮的分水嶺，過此以後，可正如秋天日子，日漸蕭條，又待霜飛雪降之後，那一切就要全給宇宙遺忘去了。　　對於秋天，所感不過如是，也許自已到了中年以後，自男有其感慨心境。至以落葉悲秋的虛弱之感，我想於我到底尙少一些緣份，現在是無法修到的。雖無五陵年少的豪情，金衣駿駒，耀眼人間；而在諷爽的天空金陽之下，精神將更煥發，把生活調整得嚴肅些，自己想來都覺得頗為安心的。甲板上  達　　一陣鑼鼓聲噹噹的敲過之後，幾個棕色臉孔，黑牙齒的「馬打」，（警察）傲然地向甲板上的角落里的幾個頹然，低沉着腦袋，手兒給被反綑着的小伙子瞟着一個得意而又輕視的眼色，裂開了血紅的嘴巴，哈哈地笑着，隨後掉轉腦袋跳上岸去了。　　小山似的龐大的輸船，　嘟的咆哮出怪刺耳的聲音來，彷彿在向人示威，腹下的機器「空隆空隆」的動着，岸上的巍巍的建築物慢慢地給丟掉在屁股之後了。　　「馬打」的輕蔑的恥笑聲，銅鑼的急促的響聲，以及輸船的刺耳的汽笛聲，……像一縷瞟渺的絲，緊緊地纏繞在這些不幸的可憐人的心靈里，便他們更加覺得難過，恥辱，悲切，悒鬱，腦袋低沈，不敢（寗可說是無興）抬起頭來瞧望南國的澄碧澈凈的藍天，輕飄的流雲，和靑蒼欲滴的林木。　　入，像看雜戲似的把他們團團地圍成一個大圈子，沒有人肯走上前去給他們解開那粗麻繩子，而且，一個個都投過來一股迫人的寒森森的鄙夷的目光，三三兩兩的嘟噥着：　　「大槪是犯盜案給送回去了」！有的人說。　　「媽的，看個子並不是連幾斤重量的東西都不能提舉的人，幹嗎要做出這種沒天良的勾當？眞是不知死活的傢伙，到　邦來　　　完　囚　，該死的囚囊！……　　人叢中有些喜歡諧謔的傢伙，衝出人叢來，在他們的臉龐上塗着黑淋淋的墨汁，「看呀，看這些不要臉的小野種！像發瘋般的叫喊着，於是，看熱鬧的人也裂開了嘴巴，格格地笑出來。　　這些不幸的人的腦袋是更加低沈下去的，他們的心靈的悒鬱，使他們失掉了反抗的性能，任憑人們的作弄，擺佈！簡直他們已變成了沒有靈魂的呆子了　　陡然間人叢中闖出來一個年紀約莫四五十歲跛了一隻左脚的老番，在這些被送回去的人的中間年紀最靑的小伙子的面前蹲下去，抬起他的腦袋很仔細地端詳着。　　「你可不是東村里的小獅子」？他皺着眉頭問，嗓音像一只嘶破的銅鑼。　　「是的。你是上社里的長興伯嗎？」這小夥子心靈里有點愕然，楞住了眼珠子呆呆地望着。　　「到底你犯了什麼官司？……」他給他解開了手腕上的粗麻繩子。　　「我是不知道的。」他茫然，在這冷辣的人羣中，陡然地得到了熱烈的安慰，使他不得不眼淚滔滔地從眼眶里滾出來了。　　「在家里種田不是好過嗎，幹嗎要跑出？」他嘆着氣，隨後又繼續地問：「你什麼時候到　呢？」　　（提起家鄕，小獅子的心像爆發的炸彈似的碎裂了，眼淚有如深山里的瀑布，源源不絕地瀉下來。他想起今年的水災的情景，在水上過了整整一個多月的生活，一家人都餓得只勝一副可怕的骨骼，他的三歲的可愛的孩子，終於給饑餓的魔鬼帶到天國里去。）　　「我是剛剛到埠的。那天在番衙門（移民局）里，紅毛鬼子向我到這里來做什麼事，我對他說來「作工」。他又問我到什麼地方去，我說「小坡」。於是，他再問我可有路費嗎，我答他「沒有，正想向親戚家借」。他就把我關起來，隔二天，不分皂白，原船給送回「唐山」了！……」　　看熱鬧的這些老番，當然明瞭紅毛鬼子這兩年來所規定下來的「　律」，這卽是所謂不容許「失業的人上岸」！於是，他們洞悉這些不幸的人來歷，靜靜地搖蕩腦袋走開了。祇有海水還在沙沙的給他門嘆着無窮的嘆息！四川山歌  江中魚作　　隔河望見牡丹開喲，喂，好朶鮮花不過來，喲喂，　　惟願天爺下大雨，喲喂，風吹牡丹過河來，喲喂。陸家染坊  代尼　　陸家染坊的店主不姓陸，姓黃。顧客們問起這緣由時，那位五十多歲的黃老闆，高聲地咳了聲嗽，但是沒有東。他說話先得打掃喉嚨，否則，他的沙啞的喉音，人家聽來是不大清切的。然後伸了伸　子，這舉動也已成了習慣，　和氣回答人家：實在不曉得了，實在不曉得了……於是用他粗大的手指抓着頭

，接着說：記得我家老大爺在的時候，已叫做陸家染坊。——大槪最初開辦這染坊的姓陸，是這樣吧？是這樣吧？老闆始終不肯說斷頭話。「那末」店堂子里常有客人來撩天，橫刺里打趣了：「現在可以叫做黃家染坊了，不是黃　的子孫做着老闆嗎？」　　店堂子里的小伙計也放肆地笑了，因爲那打趣的客人也姓黃。但是老闆不懂得這些討便宜的關節，搖着頭，正正經經地回答：「不能的，不能的，這是祖宗傳下來！你看……」彷彿老闆乾那樣粗大的食指指着檐前的招牌，「這是金字招牌，陸—家—染—坊，不能改的，不能改的！」蹣跚地推動着一百八十磅的矮身材在店堂子里踱着方步。　　老闆雖然是個誠實的粗漢子，却有一手做生意的本領。他三十歲時從老太爺手里接過來的時候，恰巧是歐戰，他把店里的現欵全數購了碇靑，在父親面前賣弄本領說：「這是個發財機會，爸爸，你瞧着吧，你瞧吧！」　　老太爺微笑着沒有回答。他知道這兒子有點傻勁，故以他把店舖早一點放手，看兒子挑上這付重担子試試，要是不行的話，老太爺還可以馬上收回來自己幹上幾年的。　　這一試老太爺放了心，那末多的碇靑都變了十倍以上的本錢。兒子覺得這一著他無論如何比老子强。「爸爸，不是嗎？發了財，發了財，以後別來顧問我，至多把賺來的賠了去！」　　但是他始終沒有賠本，陸家染坊在他手里做了二十年賺錢生意。　　雖然那方金字招牌像獺狗皮一樣地吊在檐前，店堂却不是老太爺手里那般的寒傖了。新式的櫃台，上好的漆水，可以瞧見人的面孔。靠壁新裝的櫃橱，都標着號碼，一落大派。賬台前上了黃銅的欄籽，像火車站的售票處。那位有八字鬚的兩代老賬房忙得沒有抽水烟的時候，紙煤擱在烟袋上往往一支連着一支都燒了灰。但是每個人高高興興，年底那筆花紅着實呌人不相信哩。　　老闆在店堂子里踱步，他運用做生意的本領，那股子傻勁！　　但是到了他想不通的時侯了，他接手以來沒有碰到過這種年成。踱步子，傻勁，部沒有效力；紮彩牌樓，大减價都幹過了，老闆想不透那些主顧們現在幹着什麼？陸家染坊，挺出名的，染出來的東西，永不退色，越穿越鮮潔，那是有口皆碑的。但是！那些主顧們幹什麼着了？不穿衣服？老闆笑了，沒有這道理！他想要是老頭在，看他有什麼方法？但是自己的兒子沒有比老子强，老是喊着：關了拿倒，開什麼鳥店，有的是錢，搬到上海去享福。　　老闆雖不贊成享福，但亦有「關了拿倒」之意：不過陸家染坊是祖宗傳下來，挺有名氣的老店倒了，塌祖宗的台！　　「混蛋！」他指着兒子駡，忘了咳嗽，聲音眞像一個蛋似的滾了出來，但是沒有忘了伸　子：「這是祖宗傳下來的！你想想看，你想想看，我一上手就賺了幾萬！你們洋學堂里讀些什麼書？敎敎老子關店，豈有此理，豈有此理」！　　兒子吐出舌頭榴了。他還是踱步子，或者抓着自家的頭髮，」姓陸的死鬼作怪，一定的，一定的，把招牌換了，換黃家染坊！」他吩咐店里的伙計。但是：一慢慢，待我好好點想一想，明天再說。」他衝出店門，向街上去打聽市面了。播音消息國學　　馮明權唐詩　　明遠（九六〇）上午七時半至八時半　　講題　詠懷古迹五首（補三首）　　支　東北風　際。　　西南天地間。三陜樓台淹日月。五溪衣服　雲山。　胡事主終無賴。詞客哀時且未還。庾信生平最蕭瑟。暮年辭賦動江關。（其一）　　搖落深知宋玉悲·風流儒雅亦吾師。悵望千伙一灑淚。蕭條異代不同時。江山故宅空文藻。雲雨荒台豈夢想。最是楚宮俱泯滅。舟人指點到今疑。（其二）　　蜀主低吳幸三峽。崩年亦在永安宮。翠華想像空山裏。玉殿虛無野寺中。古廟杉松巢水鶴。歲時伏蜡走村翁。武侯祠屋長鄰近。一體君臣祭祀同。（其四）特别節目　　藝聲音樂研究會　　交通（一三〇）下午五時至六時　　自由車進行曲（曹庚瑜）春之微笑（周亞俊）精兵（梁志明）臨時報吿（秦泰來）愛之古巢（戴曼如）曼持林獨奏（孔亞靑）茶花女（序曲）（梁志明）獨唱（林道南）卡門拔萃曲（文華）皇后（戴曼如）手風琴（馬維元）靴房之大將（孔亞靑）浮士德圓舞曲（馬鏡文）馬小達（分解和音）（文華）　　燕燕社　　大陸（六二〇）下午九時一刻至十時　　人面桃花（純美）蝴蝶姑娘（馬莉）西宮怨（安娜）蘇武牧羊（張珷）吹咆咆（馬莉）因爲你（純美）　　稚鳴社　　交部（一三〇〇）下午十時半至十一時半　　小桃紅（獨奏）從軍別愛（陳萍）休息五分鐘（璐玲）好朋友來了（瑛瑛）（俞微）愛情是什麼（柴瑟）自殺尙未成功（珂玲）船夫曲（斐君）賣報歌（斐虾）我要你的一切（璐玲）蘇三不要哭（沈瑛）永遠在後台（斐君）（陳萍）永遠親愛（沈玲）沈瑛）離別的姑娘（西俊）杯酒高歌（獨奏）彈詞　　邢瑞亭釵頭鳳　　惠靈（一三八〇）下午九時至十時　　開篇「紅娘寄書」，　　一色杏花十里紅，鶯鶯小姐在閨中，只爲西廂張君瑞，嬾在閨房繡女工，昨日紅娘行到西廂去，他說道張相公有病在床中，意欲前去望望他，只怕親娘家法凶，我只得寫一封書信通達張君瑞，莫把奴奴掛在胸，即便取出文房寶，十指尖尖把墨磨濃，輕輕落筆書成就，圖書花押壘重重，髮邊剪下了香雲髮，外面還繞紅綠絨，那時便把紅娘喚，你與我將書送與張相公，紅娘奉了千金命，繞過廻廊又轉東，進了柴竹門兩扇，但只見園中花木色鮮紅，一路花街砌成棋盤式，薔薇花紮就錦屏風，喜只喜白鶴海棠沿街種，老梅生得甚玲瓏，東邊種的芭蕉樹，西邊却有大梧桐，這邊種的千年君子竹，鐵芽松根對大皮松，紅娘是獨從壽仙橋上行將去，但只見小橋流水響、東，橋東一帶樹楊柳，池內荷花色未紅，鴛鴦交頸池邊伴，湖內金魚化作龍紅娘是再向朱藤棚下行將去，只見綉球花迎面又相逢，桃源洞內將身轉，仙人洞內有老人峯，玩月亭中觀夜景，自免時時戲草中，但只見鴛鴦廳造得能奇巧，假山邊種的鷄冠老少紅，見一座書房朝南造，裏邊擺設甚精工，居中一隻花梨桌，兩邊六隻細梅公，雲母天然朝外擺，文昌夫子供居中，香几上供一隻文昌鼎，連降芸櫝透九重，中間掛一幅名人畫，筆法娟妍細又工，一付對聯分左右，綾邊市裱梅箋紅，上聯是風吹楊柳條條綫，下聯是雨打桃花片片紅，看不盡書房多少景，前面已到內房中，行到床前站身定，見書生半倦睡　朧，氣喘吁吁斜靠文鴛枕，旁邊恰好少參童，相公啊，奴今奉了千金命，特地前來把信通，張生聽，笑融融，取書即刻便開封，定心仔細從頭看，裏邊寫得甚情濃，自從普救寺中遊一回，與君心下兩情濃，那年賊兵造亂孫飛虎，家母將我許配兄，蒙君竭力將兵　，白馬將軍意氣雄，萬不料家母忽地將婚悔，聞君聽說恨無窮，勸君保重身軀爲第一，莫把奴奴掛在胸，但等八月中秋晚，再使紅娘把信通，與君月下訴情衷。歌唱　　飛音社　　中西（一〇四〇）下午六時至七時　　夜深深（俞月明）鐵蹄下的歌女（姚瑤）愛情是什麼（姚莉）微微風（文良）花生米（俞月明）愛的花（姚瑶）聲聲慢（姚莉）燕雙飛（佈德）

界中爭光也。　　「凱歌」有主題歌「凱歌」，為已故一劉時代」靑年作曲家聶耳作歌並譜。　　「暴風雨一尤在蘇州眞光開映，迄巳旬日。　　應雲衛近日卸去西裝，改着中裝，有時則，中西合壁，即長其衫，而其褲是也。黄堯氏之幽默漫畫「牛鼻子」將出單行本　　黃堯氏專作之幽默漫畫「牛鼻子」早巳散見於各大圖書雜誌。牛鼻子作風，其構圖之筆觸，在漫畫界中別立一幟，以極簡煉之綫條，作出種秤活躍之姿態，生活之表情，完全不借文字為襯托，使幅面整潔萬分，可與美國之F．Fanley和瑞士之Underson為勁敵。今作者彙集原稿，挑選極幽默署，再增挿更精佳而所未曾發表過者，新印成冊，由上海福州路中市羣衆圖書公司出版，全書一槪精製，鋅版印刷。全冊四十四頁，僅售一角，聞十月十日國慶紀念日即可出版云。

1935.09.21

(Nanjing) The National Judicial Conference held its closing ceremony at 2:00 PM on the 20th. Attendees included Central Representative Wang Zhaoming, National Government Representatives Ye Chucang, Dai Chuanxian, He Yingqin, Huang Musong, and over 500 members. Chairman Ju Zheng delivered the closing address, stating that through this conference, judicial unity could be achieved, judicial improvement could be determined, which was truly gratifying, and he hoped that colleagues in the legal field would continue to contribute opinions at any time. Wang Zhaoming's address emphasized the importance of the Judicial Yuan and other organs jointly taking responsibility for the implementation of the conference's resolutions, highlighting the bright future of the judiciary, and the dependence on it for the freedom and happiness of the people's lives and property, as well as the promotion and glory of the nation. Ye Chucang's address expressed his hope that the implementation of the conference's resolutions would be carried out within the agencies under the Judicial Yuan, as most of the attendees were those who would implement them, and they had contributed their past experiences of hardship to the resolutions. The implementation of the resolutions should be smooth in the future. Member Zhang Zhiben delivered a speech on behalf of all members, expressing deep respect to the chairman, central government, and representatives of the National Government, and especially hoped that the administrative organs would assist in maintaining judicial funding and exercising judicial powers, so that the conference's resolutions could truly be implemented. The ceremony then concluded and the meeting adjourned. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

(Nanjing) The National Judicial Conference held its fifth general meeting on the morning of the 20th, attended by 159 people including Ju Zheng and Tan Zhen, and 24 observers. Mao Zuquan presided over the meeting. The meeting passed 21 proposals from the first review group, 21 from the second group, 7 from the third group, and 18 from the fourth group. The most heated discussion was on the proposal to eliminate the double collection of litigation fees and service fees at the first instance level. The former was resolved to be sent to the Judicial Yuan, and the latter to the Ministry of Justice. By this point, all 446 proposals had been discussed and completed. Then, the closing declaration was discussed and it was decided to have the presidium organize the text. After the meeting, the inaugural meeting of the China Law Society was held, passing 21 articles of the constitution. Chiang Kai-shek was elected as honorary chairman, Wang Zhaoming and eight others as honorary directors, Ju Zheng as chairman, Tan Zhen and Dai Chuanxian as vice-chairmen, Ye Chucang, Sun Ke and nine others as standing directors, Wang Longhui and ninety-five others as directors, Pan Enpei and one hundred and seven others as alternate directors, and Hong Lanyou as secretary-general. The general headquarters was established in Nanjing, with branches established in various locations. The meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM, and the closing ceremony was held at 2:00 PM in the afternoon. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

(Nanjing) The National Judicial Conference issued a declaration, divided into two points: the current situation improvement and future hopes. (A) Current Situation Improvement: The essence of the spirit of this conference lies in three points: First, the independence of judicial funding. The movement for the independence of education funding has been going on for many years and has recently begun to take effect, establishing a foundation for education. The importance of the judiciary is no less than that of education. Without sufficient funding, there is no way to plan for future progress, let alone maintain the current situation. For the sake of the people's suffering, social order, the future of the rule of law, and the national spirit, the central and provincial financial authorities should share this vision and make every effort to help achieve it. This is what the colleagues are praying for from the people of the whole country. Second, the special establishment of legal research institutions. Since the establishment of the National Government, with efforts in legislation, civil and criminal codes have gradually become complete. However, our country's substantive law has only been promulgated for a few years and can be said to still be in the process of verification. The only institutions for verification are the courts that verify trials and judgments. In addition, the amendment of procedural laws and regulations has made much progress, but whether the implementation of the procedures can still be simplified should take into account both the general common principles of the world and the special circumstances of society. Scholars from home and abroad and judicial practitioners should be brought together to conduct joint research. As a result of the conference, a legal research association was established to promote academic pursuits and explore practical experimentation to contribute to the establishment of laws. This is something that colleagues must continue to work hard on and dare not slack off. Third, the improvement of the court organization. The existing levels are complete, but the lower levels are not sufficiently established. Furthermore, the organization in the interior is more complete, while remote provinces often simplify due to poverty. Such abnormal development is not a proper organization of the judiciary. Therefore, the proposals at this conference often focus on the soundness of lower-level personnel and seek the balanced progress of courts nationwide. It is particularly important that the Judicial Yuan follow this direction and see it implemented. In addition, issues such as the improvement of prisons, the establishment of courts everywhere, the handling of political crimes, the implementation of judicial officer performance evaluations, and the rectification of the lawyer system are all numerous and difficult to list in detail. They are all crucial plans for the improvement of the current situation. (B) Future Hopes: There are two main points. First, the improvement of legal education. A person should first have character and knowledge, and then literary talent. Judicial officers come from students of law and should pay particular attention to their studies and character in peacetime. Therefore, in the future, legal education should emphasize character cultivation in addition to legal principles, so that they can become all-round talents, apply what they have learned, and conduct practical training in legal application and judicial practice to become independent and practical judicial officers. This is for the sake of emphasizing both legal theory and application, and it is what is hoped for from the legal education authorities. Second, the abolition of consular jurisdiction. The abolition of unequal treaties is a consistent demand of our people. Among the unequal treaties, consular jurisdiction is the most serious. However, Japan, Turkey, Siam and other countries have precedents for the abolition of this legal right. Recently, codes have gradually been completed. If courts and prisons in all provinces can be established everywhere and reach perfection, then the scale of the judiciary will become a backing for diplomacy. Therefore, the resolutions of this conference aim to improve various facilities and save legal rights. However, the responsibilities of colleagues are limited to the judiciary, and this depends on the joint efforts of the people of the country. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

Song Zheyuan Arrives in Beiping, Taking Office Today, Plans to Visit Chahar After Taking Office, Wang Shuchang Went to Baoding Yesterday 1

(Tianjin) At 9:15 AM on the 20th, Song Zheyuan, accompanied by Qin Dechun, Xiao Zhenying, Zhang Zizhong, commander of the 38th Division of the 29th Army, and Zhang Yunrong, commander of the Chahar Garrison, went to Beiping. They arrived at the Beiping-Tianjin Garrison Headquarters at 11:00 AM on the 21st to handle affairs. Qin Dechun said that Song would take office on the 21st. The deployment locations of the various units of the 29th Army had not yet been determined. Song intended to leave the organization of the health garrison headquarters unchanged for the time being, and would reorganize it later according to the regulations prescribed by the central government. He himself would return to Chahar after Song took office. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Beiping) Since Song had arrived in Beiping, Wang Shuchang went to Baoding this morning, stayed for a short day, and then went to Hankou to see Chiang in Sichuan to report everything. He would also visit Mount Emei for about a month before going to Beijing to take office. Song Zheyuan and more than 300 military and political officials went to the station to see Wang off. Wang said that he would meet with Wan Fulin in Baoding before heading south. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Beiping) Song arrived in Beiping from Tianjin this afternoon, accompanied by Qin Dechun and Xiao Kuoying. Military and political organs here gave a grand welcome, including Yuan Liang, Bao Wenyue, Shao Wenkai, Zhang Zizhong, Feng Zhizhi'an, Zhang Yunrong, the chiefs of the garrison headquarters, and more than 300 representatives from the silver merchants and other sectors. Security teams and military police were stationed as guards inside and outside the station. Song said that he had originally planned to come to Beiping on the 15th, but was delayed due to a cold. The rumor that he had made demands to the central government was inaccurate. He would take office at the headquarters tomorrow afternoon without holding a ceremony. There would be no increase in personnel at the headquarters. The defense of Tianjin had not yet been discussed with the 32nd Army. He would discuss the defense along the Beiping-Tianjin line after taking office. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Beiping) Qin Dechun arrived in Beiping with Song this morning. According to him, he would stay in Beiping for a few days and then return to Zhangjiakou. More than 1,000 security team members have been sent to suppress the bandits near Yanqing, and it is hoped that they can be eliminated. (Special dispatch, 20th)

Wang Kemin Answers the Call of Commander Tada, Departs Tianjin That Night to Go South to Beijing 2

(Tianjin) Wang Kemin visited Sakai Takashi, Chief of Staff of the Japanese Garrison, in the early morning of the 20th, and visited Tada Hayao, Japanese Commander, in the afternoon to express his farewell and resignation. He took the Jinpu express train south at 10:20 PM that night. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Beiping) According to reports, Wang Kemin went to mourn Zhang Zhitian at 9:00 AM this morning. At 11:00 AM, he and Gu Rugeng went to Zhang Yuan to return the call of Tada, commander of the Japanese garrison, and had a one-hour meeting. Cheng Ke hosted a banquet at noon, and Tada hosted Wang in the evening at 7:00 PM. Wang departed south to Beijing at 10:00 PM that night. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng took the Pingyu train to Tianjin at 5:50 AM this morning, arriving around 9:00 AM. After getting off the train, he went to see Wang Kemin to attend the meeting between Wang and Tada. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng went to Tianjin on the morning of the 20th and accompanied Wang Kemin to visit Tada at noon. After finishing the business, he returned to Tangshan. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

(Nanjing) After the conclusion of the Beiping Political Reorganization Committee, all important cases and files have been brought to Beijing by Xu Xiuzhi of the Ministry of Interior. For other cases related to Hebei Province and the Military Branch Committee, Xu presented a request to the Executive Yuan, which approved the establishment of a file storage office with a very small organizational scope, employing only two first-class clerks, eight second-class clerks, ten staff members, and eight workers, with a monthly budget of 2,000 yuan. It is expected to be abolished after six months and placed under the jurisdiction of the Military Branch Committee. (Special dispatch, 20th)

Dutch Envoy Visits Mausoleum Yesterday 3

(Nanjing) Dutch Ambassador Frans, accompanied by Dao Fan, section chief of the Protocol Bureau of the National Government, and the director of the external affairs department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, led his staff to the tomb of the Premier on the 20th to pay respects and present flowers. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Nanjing) Dutch Ambassador Frans, accompanied by Secretary Weidebaosi, went to the Mausoleum Park at 4:00 PM on the afternoon of the 20th, escorted by Qu Chang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, to pay respects and offer wreaths. He returned to the city at 5:00 PM and held a tea party at the embassy at 6:00 PM to host officials from our various agencies and diplomatic and consular officials from various countries stationed in Nanjing. Dozens of people attended and the party ended at 8:00 PM. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

Legislative Yuan Resolution, President Sun Discusses Central Political Situation and International Trends 4

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its 29th meeting on the morning of the 20th, attended by 70 members including He Sui. President Sun Ke and Secretary-General Liang Hancao discussed the following items: 1. The general budget of local ordinary income and expenditure of the Weihaiwei Management Office for the 24th year of the Republic of China. Resolved: passed as is. 2. Posthumous recognition of the Republic of China's 21st law: The Ministry of Interior's handling of nationality issues has considerable room for discretion and consideration of the circumstances, and it was agreed to explicitly state this, lest it be too rigid and difficult to implement. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

(Nanjing) After the Yuan meeting on the morning of the 20th, Sun Ke met with reporters from the Central News Agency to discuss the central political situation and international trends. Sun stated that the central government convened the Sixth Plenary Session in accordance with the Party Constitution to resolve matters to be prepared before the Fifth National Congress, such as the draft constitution, which is still under study by the central government. Whether it will be submitted to the Congress will also depend on the decision of the plenary session. The date of the Congress will not be delayed again. There has been no news regarding whether the national economy and the implementation of currency inflation will be discussed at the Congress. The rumor that Yu, Cai Yuanpei, Li Shizeng, and others jointly proposed a fixed deadline for the implementation of constitutional government is untrue. When reporters asked about the possibility of the outbreak of war between Italy and Abyssinia, Sun continued that the Italian prime minister has now become unable to back down, and the dispute may be difficult to avoid. After the outbreak of war, Britain, in order to maintain the credibility of the League of Nations and its own interests, will be drawn into the vortex. This is evidenced by the British government's recent concentration of the Far East Fleet in Singapore, preparing to sail to the Mediterranean, which is even more credible. France, because of its powerful enemy Germany, will also follow Italy's example and threaten Austria. Its situation is similar to that of Britain, and it will also help Britain to protest, as a condition for future exchanges. After the outbreak of war, our only hope is to maintain neutrality, and we especially hope that war can be avoided, because our country is not only unable to take care of itself, but also unable to save itself and has no ability to help others. Finally, regarding the arrival of Leith-Ross in China, Sun did not want to express any opinion. When asked whether the Foreign Affairs and Finance Committees of the Legislative Yuan would invite him to the Yuan to exchange views after Leith-Ross arrived in Beijing, Sun replied that it had not been decided. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

(Nanjing) Legislative member Deng Zhexi returned to Beijing on the 20th after visiting Feng Yuxiang in Tai'an from Beiping. After the Legislative Yuan meeting, he met with Sun Ke to report. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

Xu Shiying Returns to Beijing 5

(Nanjing) Xu Shiying, chairman of the Relief Committee for Disaster Relief in Northern Jiangsu, returned to Beijing on the morning of the 20th. According to him, the places visited were Feng, Pei, Tong, and Pi counties, with Pi County being the most severely affected. The water depth reached two to three zhang. The water level in Suqian and Shuyang has not subsided, and Guanyun is still feared to be affected. The more than 10,000 yuan carried for relief have been handed over to local officials for distribution. The local authorities have formulated resettlement and relief measures. After meeting with Chen Guofu for consultations, Xu will go to Shanghai. (20th)

(Nanjing) Xu Shiying arrived in Beijing on the morning of the 20th and visited Director Wang at noon to report on the disaster situation in northern Jiangsu, who agreed to raise funds. He visited Finance Minister Kong in the afternoon to check on his throat ailment. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

(Nanjing) Xu Shiying said that the disaster area in northern Jiangsu includes Fengpei, Tong, Pi, Su, and Shu counties, covering approximately 2,500 square kilometers, with 900,000 disaster victims. Pi County is the most severely affected. Although the water level in Xuzhou has stabilized, the trend cannot be predicted. Guanyun may also be affected. In short, if the breach in Shandong is not blocked for a day, Jiangsu will not be able to escape the threat of the Yellow River for a day. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

Yellow River Diversion Drains Into the Sea Through the Six Ditches, Downstream Water Level Rises Sharply 6

(Qingjiangpu) The Yellow River water is diverted into the sea through the six ditches. The four gates of Shuyang Qianji have been blocked, and ships are detouring. East of Tangjiang in the lower reaches of the six ditches, Deng Xianghai and others from Shuyang, Guanyun, and Lian counties are supervising the people to rush to repair the dangerous sections. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Xuzhou) Hai'an reported that the water level in the lower reaches of the Six Ditches River has risen sharply. The Donghai County government has mobilized a large number of people to cut reeds in the Qiangwei River to facilitate water flow. There are still many dangerous works on the embankments along the river in Shuyang and Guanyun, and the people in various places along the river are working hard to prevent them. (Special dispatch, 20th)

Several Zhang of the Salt River Sluice Gate Dam Collapsed

(Qingjiangpu) Today, the water level dropped by six centimeters to 36.877 meters. The water level at Yaowan rose by one inch to 264 inches. The water level at Qingjiang remained at 246 inches. News from Suqian: Several zhang of the Huaiyin Guanhe sluice gate dam collapsed, and the situation is very precarious. Xun Yuan Liutang Li Da has reported to the Huaipi section to request instructions on how to deal with the situation. The water level in the sluice gate has now increased to three zhang and four chi and two cun. (Special dispatch, 20th)

Service Corps Allocated 100 People

(Xuzhou) The Commissioner's Office selected young people from the disaster victims to form a post-disaster service group of 120 people, 20 from Tong and Pei counties, 90 from Pi County, and 10 from Feng County. They are scheduled to gather at the office for a week of training on the first of next month and then set off to serve in the disaster area. (Special dispatch, 20th)

Hubei Disaster Relief Association Distributes First Batch of Charitable Relief To Focus on Relief for Eight Counties Including Tianmen, Zhongxiang and Other Places Also Suffer from Floods

(Hankou) The Flood Relief Association and the Charity Relief Association held a joint meeting on the 20th to distribute the first batch of 150,000 yuan of charitable relief. It is heard that the relief will be specifically allocated to eight counties including Tianmen, Hanchuan, Hanyang, Zhongxiang, Yicheng, Xiangyang, Shishou, and Songzi. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Hankou) The Provincial Government telegraphed the Central Relief Association on the 20th, stating that sixteen counties including Zhongxiang have suffered from floods again, and the replanted autumn crops have all been submerged. Please allocate a large sum of money to relieve the disaster victims. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Hankou) The Headquarters ordered the Provincial Government on the 20th to coordinate relief for flood and drought disasters. (Special dispatch, 20th)

Beining Railway Orders Passenger Car Trains from South Manchuria Railway Company, Value 1.19 Million Japanese Yen, Yin Tong Returned to Tianjin from Shenyang Yesterday 7

(Tianjin) The Beining Railway Bureau announced that, in view of the significant progress in Japanese-made railway vehicles in recent years, the bureau has submitted a report to the Central Government for approval to order two new-style passenger car trains from the South Manchuria Railway Company. Including spare vehicles, the total includes three high-class dining cars, two first-class sleeping and lounge cars, three second-class sleeping cars, seven second-class passenger cars, and four baggage and postal cars. The total cost of the cars is 1.29 million Japanese yen. The contract was formally signed on the 19th and delivery will be made within one year. These vehicles are all new-style, with observation platforms and air-conditioning in the dining cars and sleeping cars. Xie Zhen, director of the Tangshan factory of the railway, will, together with the mechanical department, send personnel and assistants to supervise the manufacturing during the manufacturing period. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Beiping) Yin Tong went to Dalian on the 16th of this month to order two new-style passenger car trains from the South Manchuria Railway Company, valued at more than 1.38 million Japanese yen. The contract was formally signed in Dalian on the 19th and delivery will be made within one year. Yin has completed his business in Dalian and will return to Tianjin today. (Special dispatch, 20th)

(Tianjin) Yin Tong returned to Tianjin from Shenyang early in the morning. When he returned from Shanhaiguan by train, he stopped at Luan County, Changli, Tangshan and other places along the way to inspect the road affairs. (Special dispatch, 20th)

Tianjin Kidnapping Case, 14 Criminals Confess Without Denial 8

(Tianjin) In the major kidnapping case in the British Concession of Tianjin, 14 male and female criminals have been arrested so far. They have been questioned by the British Public Works Bureau and have confessed without denial. There were eleven cases, twelve people were torn to pieces after receiving ransoms. The victims were killed first, then ransoms demanded. The operation was quick and discreet, making it difficult for outsiders to know. It is heard that the British Public Works Bureau will hand them over to the Public Security Bureau for legal action after completing the procedures. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

Current Affairs Commentary

Unified Disaster Relief Efforts - Dou 9

The autumn moon is coming to an end. The flood season is gradually passing. The flood terror that has been lingering in people's hearts can almost be eliminated along with the summer heat and epidemics. The anxious mood of the past few months can now be slightly relieved. This is what we are comforted by. However, remembering the tragic impression of the past, it is also the path to future disasters. If we do not take the time to think about the pain and plan for ways to ensure safety, the dangerous situation will re-emerge in a blink of an eye, and there will be another sacrifice. Isn't it regrettable? Moreover, there are mourners everywhere with little to rely on. The cold is gradually increasing, and their clothes are incomplete. The pain of wandering and separation increases with each passing day. Therefore, disaster relief work today is not only impossible to slack off, but should also be prepared to intensify. This is what people across the country should pay absolute attention to.

Regarding the implementation of disaster relief matters, this newspaper has repeatedly contributed its critical remarks. Furthermore, Mr. Baker, advisor to the National Government Relief Commission, wrote a special letter, acknowledging this as the only urgent task at present. Public opinion has a need to repeatedly state this. Mr. Baker also suggested many points for reference. We are grateful to Mr. Baker for focusing on the disaster situation as a foreign guest, and at the same time, we also feel that disaster relief work does not shy away from detailed discussions. I will not hesitate to elaborate and discuss Mr. Baker's suggestions one by one.

Summarizing Mr. Baker's opinions, there are two main points. One is unified and exclusive power. The second is to organize work relief. The lack of unity in disaster relief affairs has long been criticized by insightful people. Overlapping agencies only create an excuse for shirking responsibility after the fact, and rarely obtain the effectiveness of responding to emergencies. In the situation where provinces act on their own, it is especially easy for conflicts of interest to occur. After all, a river passes through several provinces. Since there is no clear boundary to divide, although it is avoided to take care of one thing and lose sight of another, the misunderstandings caused by this are at least enough to hinder water control facilities. Furthermore, engineering projects have expansion and contraction, and the narrow areas have dangerous and easy sections. How to estimate, how to adjust, all depend on the highest authority for the overall setting. Planning the transportation of materials and the allocation of manpower must be handled in a unified manner to achieve a balanced layout. If the power can be concentrated in one agency, and under its command and supervision, it can be assigned to the agencies according to their duties and assigned responsibilities, then the efficiency of the work can be seen, and unnecessary disputes can be avoided. Organizing work relief is consistent with the meaning of considering both aspects. With the prevalence of disaster victims today and the shortage of relief funds, there is too little porridge for too many monks, and it is difficult to achieve universal coverage. Furthermore, the days to come are long, so how can we continue? If the strong among the disaster victims are assigned to construction projects, it will directly fulfill the responsibility of saving the disaster victims. Indirectly, it is also a strategy to promote the progress of water conservancy projects. For women and children who cannot endure the arduous work, they may be assigned to easy tasks such as hammering stones and paving roads. Then, even without the support of men, they can support themselves by their own strength. Isn't this better than sitting idly by and waiting for help?

Yesterday, the newspaper reported that the Economic Commission considered that blocking the breaches and rebuilding the levees of the Yangtze River and the Yellow River were urgent tasks. It has formulated seven outlines and ordered the Yangtze River and Yellow River Water Commissions to plan the construction separately. Furthermore, the Tongpei Commissioner's Office is also selecting young people from the disaster victims to form labor service groups in the disaster area. The authorities are already implementing unified disaster relief and organizing work relief separately. It is hoped that all relief organizations will cooperate closely and that people from all over the country will actively donate to jointly promote the advancement of disaster relief work.

Geneva and Rome Relay Messages, Italy's Attitude Suddenly Changes 10

Suggestions Can Be Seen as a Basis for Discussion, France, Britain, and Italy Liaise Again Yesterday

(Geneva) The views held by Italian officials regarding the recommendations made by the five-nation committee of the League of Nations Administrative Council have recently been relatively favorable, and it is believed that these recommendations can be used as a basis for discussing various technical issues. The fact that this recommendation is powerless to modernize the administrative powers exercised by the Emperor of Abyssinia, and therefore advocates limiting his sovereignty, seems to be better understood, and it is believed that this is to satisfy Italy. As for this recommendation, advocating that Abyssinia hire foreign consultants to assist, is indeed feasible, but Italy will naturally be difficult to accept if these consultants are not allowed to be Italian personnel. Some optimists believe that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's non-response to this recommendation indicates that he has adopted a more moderate policy. Italian Representative Aloisi met with French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval this morning, after which Laval had a long conversation with British Minister Without Portfolio Eden. (Havas dispatch, 20th)

(Rome) People here now believe that if the recommendations of the Five-Nation Committee are satisfactorily revised, Italy can accept them as a basis for discussion. A responsible person told a Reuters reporter that the current recommendations are unacceptable, and we cannot consider them unless they are actively revised. However, it is unknown whether Geneva can make such satisfactory revisions. (Reuters dispatch, 20th)

(Rome) Today, a responsible spokesperson claimed that Italy would never accept the recommendations of the Five-Nation Special Committee. Italy's policy has not changed, and we cannot agree to jointly manage Abyssinia with other countries. There is one good thing in the report, which is that it recognizes that the Abyssinians cannot govern themselves. Italy's firm attitude does not mean that Rome will not study the recommendations of the Five-Nation Special Committee. Although Italians believe that a compromise cannot be reached because of this, they still regard the recommendations as some basis for discussion. (Reuters dispatch, 19th)

(Geneva) This place is currently quietly awaiting the responses from the Italian and Abyssinian governments regarding the recommendations of the Five-Nation Committee. Some sources say that the Italian government is currently carefully considering the consequences of rejecting this recommendation. According to a Geneva dispatch from the French Concorde newspaper, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will not reply for two or three weeks, in order to consult with Britain and France. At the same time, the Five-Nation Committee will consider the steps to be taken after that without receiving a reply. If Italy rejects its recommendations, the Administrative Council will have to adopt sanctions in accordance with Article 15 of the Covenant, if all means of mediation have failed. (Reuters dispatch, 20th)

(Paris) According to a Geneva dispatch from the Concorde newspaper, when British Representative Eden spoke with French Prime Minister Laval this morning, he stated that the British government considers the recommendations of the Five-Nation Special Committee to be the extreme limit of concessions to Italy, and the League of Nations' final word to Italy. (Reuters dispatch, 19th)

(Geneva) The Five-Nation Special Committee held a short meeting today. Chairman Madariaga reported on the situation of handing over the memorandum of recommendations to the Italian and Abyssinian representatives. He then assumed that Saturday and Sunday would be the date for the next meeting. It is expected that the Italian government's reply will not be received until after the Italian cabinet has held a meeting. The committee members have all agreed to keep the recommendations absolutely confidential, but the leaks to the outside world are still relatively detailed, so this was discussed at today's meeting. It was decided that there was no way to think about this. While the Italian and Abyssinian replies are pending, the Special Committee will take the opportunity to consider the second step that should be taken. If the Italian government rejects the recommendations, the Administrative Council must meet and act in accordance with Article 19 of the League of Nations Covenant, which stipulates that sanctions should be implemented if all methods of mediation have been exhausted. (Reuters dispatch, 19th)

Intention to Withdraw Libyan Reinforcements to Avoid British Sanctions, but Britain Cannot Currently Provide Such Assurance 11

(Geneva) How the Italian government will respond to the recommendations of the Five-Power Committee is something no one dares to say for certain. However, it is heard that the Italian government has already inquired with several countries about their opinions on the sanctions issue. The actions of the British fleet have undoubtedly made a profound impression in Rome. It is heard that the Italian government is preparing to withdraw reinforcements to Libya in exchange for a firm guarantee from the British government regarding sanctions. Mussolini has repeatedly stated that Italy will regard military sanctions as an act of war, but he has been less outspoken about economic sanctions. If the League of Nations orders the implementation of such sanctions, Italy will apparently not regard it as a harmful action. (Reuters, 20th)

(London) According to reliable sources, the use of force and economic sanctions against Italy would have a significant impact. If Britain could guarantee not to impose military and economic sanctions on Italy, then Italy could often rescind its naval precautions in the Mediterranean. However, British political figures believe that Britain cannot currently provide such a guarantee, because future changes in circumstances may require Britain to take action, and it should not be restricted in advance. Furthermore, political figures believe that the British cabinet is currently only considering economic actions, such as lifting the ban on the transport of munitions to Abyssinia, banning the export of munitions to Italy, and severing trade relations with Italy. The current inclination of the British government is not only unwilling to soften its current attitude but also to strengthen the attitude of the central government. However, Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant, if it is to be strictly enforced, must be carried out jointly by the member states of the League of Nations, which is again and again declared by official sources. (Havas, 19th)

Britain and France Fully Agree that Sanctions are Limited to Economic Measures, Mediterranean Fleet Actions Cause Concern 12

(Paris) Although France still hopes that Mussolini will give the League of Nations a satisfactory response, it is now watching Italy's preparations for war with deep concern. The actions of the British fleet in the Mediterranean have given rise to various speculations, but responsible observers all say that if sanctions must be implemented against Italy in the future, they will only be carried out by League of Nations organizations. From the looks of it, the careful talks between Britain and France have so far been limited to economic sanctions, which is to refuse all loans to Italy. According to general opinion, Britain and France are now in complete agreement on this action. Furthermore, according to evening newspapers, military sanctions will definitely not be approved by a majority of French cabinet members. (Reuters, 19th)

(Paris) Although French newspapers all express sympathy towards Italy, the firm attitude of Britain has also had a backlash, so most newspapers are now asking Mussolini to accept the recommendations of the Five-Power Committee, not to go to extremes, and not to destroy peace. The "Paris Daily" warns Italy that although the League of Nations will never reach an agreement on military sanctions, there are still very effective economic sanctions that will eventually strike Italy. It would be wise for Mussolini to accept this recommendation, because this recommendation in fact cedes all of Abyssinia's territory to Mussolini, only formally preserving Abyssinia's sovereignty, so that the League of Nations does not lose face. After a few years, Italy can control Abyssinia's finances, politics, and economy under the guise of international supervision, thereby occupying the entire country. (National News Agency, 19th)

(London) Telegraphs received by Reuters from Gibraltar and other Mediterranean ports are sufficient to prove that the current naval activity in the Mediterranean is unprecedented. There is still no news of the number of warships in Malta harbor. Currently stationed in Gibraltar and other Mediterranean ports are a total of fourteen battleships, two battlecruisers, fourteen cruisers, twenty-nine destroyers, eleven minesweepers, two aircraft carriers, and one hospital ship. The battleships are the HMS Courageous (29,150 tons), HMS Revenge (29,150 tons), HMS Warspite (31,000 tons), and HMS Barham (31,000 tons). The battlecruisers are HMS Hood (41,200 tons), which is the largest ship in the British Navy, and HMS Renown (33,000 tons). The aircraft carriers are HMS Glorious (22,500 tons) and HMS Eagle (22,500 tons). The hospital ship is the HMS Maine. (Reuters, 19th)

Gibraltar: British military authorities published a notice stating that in certain situations, all building lights will be extinguished uniformly. Residents may prepare candles, but only those whose light cannot penetrate outdoors. (National News Agency, 20th)

(Paris) The "Paris Echo" reports from London that the British government firmly believes that Britain is sufficient to cut off Italy's oil supply when necessary. The recent movements of the British Navy are intended to achieve this. Once the Suez Canal is closed, the oil supply from both the Persian Gulf and Abadan will be cut off. At the same time, troops are being sent to defend the coast of Palestine and Haifa, so that Iraq's oil cannot be utilized by the Italians. Even if Italian troops can land on the coast of Palestine, the British will not find it difficult to defend the oil wells of Beersheba, preventing them from falling into Italian hands. Currently, Britain and Turkey are conducting negotiations in order to block the Dardanelles when necessary, blocking Italy's path to purchasing oil from Soviet Russia. (National News Agency, 20th)

Abyssinia Receives League of Nations Recommendations, Mobilization Conference Opens in the Palace 13

Addis Ababa: The recommendations of the Five-Power Committee were officially accepted here yesterday. The Emperor's final decision still needs to be made in a few days, but except for strategic reasons, it will certainly not be rejected. Today, a meeting was held in the Emperor's palace to discuss several issues related to mobilization. The Emperor also received military leaders who had arrived from various provinces. These troops have come here to be equipped with new rifles before heading to the front lines. (National News Agency, 20th)

Addis Ababa: According to news here today, Abyssinia expects Italy to attack simultaneously on five fronts. The first is the northwest route, attacking from Gondar. The second is the northern route, attacking from Asmara. The third is the eastern route of Assab, where Italy may use air power as an aid. The fourth route is the southern route, the Walwal where the Italian-Abyssinian dispute began. The fifth is from the Italian Somaliland side, advancing straight towards Addis Ababa along the Webi Shebeli River. Abyssinia today is also prepared to increase its defensive strength threefold on these five fronts, and may even launch a counterattack against Italian Somaliland. (National News Agency, 19th)

Addis Ababa: The Emperor is now preparing to issue a general mobilization order. Local chieftains are busy organizing 1.5 million strong warriors to resist the Italian army on five fronts. The Emperor is now waiting for news of Italy's rejection of the League of Nations mediation plan or the crossing of the border by Italian troops before issuing an order to resist. (National News Agency, 19th)

Thirty-Five Thousand Italian Troops, Unknown Destination, Attack on Egypt Impossible 14

(Rome) Two Italian divisions, a total of 35,000 men, are now unknown to their destination. One division is the Cossaria Division, and the other is the Assietta Division. Originally stationed in the area bordering France, they departed from Genoa aboard eighteen transport ships, ostensibly heading for East Africa. The first ship, the "Piemonte," set sail on September 7th, and the last ship, the "Lombardia," set sail on September 18th. Currently, at least eleven ships should have reached the Suez Canal, but so far, none have arrived at Port Said. This army may be heading to Tripoli and Benghazi, or the Dodecanese Islands in the Aegean Sea, but responsible parties deny that troops have been sent to North Africa, and Tripoli and Benghazi have not reported the arrival of troops. If the two divisions are indeed heading to North Africa, their purpose may be to threaten Egypt, but military opinion is almost unanimous that Egypt has more than 400 miles of waterless desert, so an attack on Egypt is almost impossible, and a large number of vehicles would be needed to transport the troops, and it would be difficult to gather so many vehicles at once. Furthermore, Italian troops passing through the desert would be at risk of being arbitrarily bombed by enemy aircraft. Today, the Stampa newspaper published a responsible article explaining that western Egypt has an impenetrable sandy barrier that can avoid attack. If this army is not going to North Africa, then it may be going to the Dodecanese Islands, but the purpose of this move is still perplexing. The islands are closer to Egypt, Palestine, and Cyprus than to any Italian port, but there is no news of troops arriving in Rhodes, which is quite surprising. Reuters reporters inquired with responsible parties about the whereabouts of the army, but the spokesman refused to see them and only said that the actions of our army are not intended against Britain or any other European country. People here all believe that the two divisions have been sent to Benghazi. (Reuters, 20th)

(Rome) The situation in the Italian-Abyssinian dispute seems to be rapidly trending towards extremes. A responsible spokesman stated yesterday that the country finds the movements of the British fleet very strange. At the same time, Italian troops are still being rapidly transported to East Africa. Yesterday, two transport ships carrying 4,000 tons of war materials departed from Naples for Massawa. Today, three more ships full of soldiers set sail for East Africa. There are ten ships in the port that are currently raising steam and waiting to depart, five of which can carry more than 2,000 soldiers. (Reuters, 20th)

(Rome) War is imminent. The situation in Italy is tense today. The country believes that the Five-Power Committee's compromise plan will definitely be rejected by Italy, so all that remains is to order an attack. Today, it is learned that Italy is psychologically prepared for a conflict with Britain. Travelers on the coast report that all places vulnerable to attack have been prepared for air defense. At the same time, large numbers of Italian troops have arrived in Italian Libya, Eritrea, and Somaliland. Newspapers are also trying to make the people aware of the possibility of an Anglo-Italian war. Gaeda, the editor of the "Italian People's Newspaper," stated that the recent arguments in British newspapers are "a declaration of determination to wage war against Italy." However, British officials here deny that British expatriates have been advised to leave Italy. Most notably, today the government ordered the establishment of a committee of sixteen people to specifically handle issues arising from belligerent and neutral countries during wartime. According to news from London, the British Steamship Company has changed the maiden voyage route of its new ship, the "Stradella," and will not stop at any Italian ports in the Mediterranean. However, the company did not announce whether this move was instructed by the British government. From Paris, it is said that Britain has deployed defenses in Mauritius as a naval base in the Red Sea. Furthermore, all family members of British officers stationed in India who are currently on leave in Britain have been advised by the government to postpone their return to India. The government has not explained this move, but it is likely that the officers there will soon be transferred elsewhere. News from Djibouti today states that Britain has set up barracks in British Somaliland and adjacent to Abyssinia. From this, it can be seen that Britain is preparing for Italy to invade Abyssinia and has begun to prevent disturbances from affecting the British border. (National News Agency, 19th)

U.S. Policy Adheres to the Pact of Paris, Denies Recall of Fleet to the Atlantic 15

(New York) Secretary of State Hull broadcast his speech on peace procedures today, stating that the U.S. government will continue to base its policy on the Kellogg-Briand Pact and hopes that other related countries will abide by their obligations as signatories. The U.S. government is closely monitoring the development of the current dispute between Italy and Abyssinia and is willing to continue to do its best in every possible way to promote peace. (Reuters, 19th)

(Washington) The State Department and the Navy Department formally denied today that a report by the French News Agency that the United States was considering moving part of the Pacific Fleet back to the Atlantic to protect merchant ships. Secretary of State Hull also stated that Secretary of the Navy Swanson had asked to announce on his behalf that the various rumors were contrary to Secretary Swanson's statement. (National News Agency, 19th)

(Washington) Secretary of the Navy Swanson today directed the Munitions Control Board to convene a meeting next Tuesday, which is a prelude to the implementation of the U.S. Neutrality Act. The U.S. Munitions Control Board is organized by the Secretary of War, Secretary of the Navy, Secretary of Commerce, Secretary of the Treasury, and Secretary of State. Officials from each department are currently compiling a list of war materials to stipulate war materials prohibited for export. (National News Agency, 19th)

European Funds Gradually Flee to the U.S., Actively Selling British Bonds 16

(London) With no sign of a peaceful resolution to the Italian-Abyssinian crisis, European funds are gradually fleeing to the United States for safety. The price of the U.S. dollar rose sharply today to $4.915625, due to the increased demand for dollars in the fall business season, as well as speculative purchases. Today's gold transaction value was 61,000 pounds, presumably due to private investors preparing to transport gold to the U.S. Britain has a more direct relationship in the Italian-Abyssinian crisis, so the pound is also affected by the war panic. European countries are actively selling British bonds, especially Paris, which has weakened the price of the pound. The British authorities are trying to maintain the exchange rate and selling francs at a price of 74.68. After news that the Italian attitude had eased slightly, the pound rebounded, but the market situation is still extremely uneasy. (Reuters, 20th)

Italy's Gold Reserves Decrease, French Bank Loans Italy 400 Million Francs 17

(Rome) According to the latest report from the Bank of Italy, cash reserves have decreased from 4,704,500,000 lire to 4,563,000,000 lire, foreign currency reserves have decreased from 476,000,000 lire to 432,000,000 lire, and the amount of paper currency in circulation has increased from 14,000,000,000 lire to 14,235,000,000 lire. (Havas, 19th)

(Paris) The Bank of France has loaned the Italian government 400 million francs, using French government bonds worth 1 billion francs as collateral. These bonds flowed into Italy due to the recent financial emergency decree. The Italian government originally wanted to exchange these bonds for cash but was ultimately rejected. This loan is only to prevent the Italian National Bank from selling these bonds on the market, causing the price of the bonds to plummet. The Paris bond market fell all day yesterday, apparently still affected by this transaction. (National News Agency, 20th)

Greece's Difficult Situation, Britain and Italy Each Want to Utilize Greek Ports 18

(Rome) It is heard here that four British battleships, eight armored cruisers, fourteen light cruisers, fifty-four destroyers, and two aircraft carriers will conduct maneuvers in Greek territorial waters on September 25th, which has caused great indignation. Officials believe that this move directly threatens the Adriatic coast, so the Italian government will lodge a strong protest. The Greek government's claim that the treaty of 1825 stipulates that Britain guarantees the independence of Greece has only increased Rome's indignation. Rome claims that no one is threatening the independence of Greece, except Britain. However, Greece's attitude has caused great unease in political circles here. These political circles are greatly panicked by the unexpected turn of events in the Greek restoration issue and deeply fear that once the restoration is realized, the British external affairs will be able to influence Greek policy even more, because the marriage of Duke of Kent and Princess Marina has established a connection between the Greek and British royal families. (National News Agency, 19th)

Athens: The Greek government has repeatedly protested the intrusion of Italian warships into Greek seaports to no avail. Today, the government ordered that henceforth, if Italian warships intrude into seaports without the permission of the authorities, then Greece will send ships to closely monitor the actions of the Italian ships. (National News Agency, 20th)

Athens: The deployment of Italian naval and land forces in the Dodecanese Islands west of Italian-controlled Asia Minor has caused extreme unease in the Greek government. The Greek government receives reports almost daily of troops landing on Lagonia and Rhodes. Rhodes is the largest island in the Dodecanese Islands. It is said that the Italians are now also developing Leros Island to make it an important naval base. In addition to oil already being unloaded on the island, there are also two cannons. These cannons were moved from Kos Island. The cabinet received an urgent telegram from Foreign Minister Maximos from Geneva and immediately convened a meeting to discuss the position of current international developments. It was resolved to protest again against the unauthorized entry of Italian warships into Greek ports. The Greek fleet has also left Thessaloniki and is heading towards Istanbul. (National News Agency, 19th)

Athens: A squadron of British aircraft, including ten large seaplanes, is scheduled to fly over Greek skies tomorrow to Egypt. The Greek authorities have permitted them to land in Phalerum or Mirabello on the Greek island of Crete in the Mediterranean. (Havas, 20th)

Spanish Military Reinforces Defenses, Aids Gibraltar's Rear 19

Madrid: Spain has concentrated its troops in the south, apparently to aid the British military position in Gibraltar and to prevent any troops from landing on Spanish territory to attack the British army's rear. Today, it was also learned that reinforcements have been sent to Ceuta in Spanish Morocco. Officials now fear that the turmoil in the Mediterranean will lead to a general mobilization of the Spanish army. (National News Agency, 19th)

Germany's Military Spending Financed by Industrialists and Financiers 20

(New York) The New Republic weekly published today an article by renowned American political and economic writer Krepsen, which stated that the sources of funds for Germany's rearmament are the country's industrialists, financiers, and labor unions. German Economics Minister Schacht forced industrialists to purchase treasury bonds to the huge sum of US$250,000,000, and anyone who disobeyed would be subjected to detention. Schacht also ordered savings banks to purchase these treasury bonds. According to reports, before the global economic panic, Germany had US$500,000,000 in cash reserves. When Hitler came to power, there was also US$100,000,000, which is a loss of US$75,000,000. According to Krepsen's estimates, Germany's military spending in recent years has been more than US$125,000,000. (National News Agency, 19th)

Bulgaria Holds Large-Scale Army Maneuvers, First Time Since the European War 21

Bulgarian Capital: Large-scale army maneuvers have been held here in recent days. Last week, there were cavalry exercises, and yesterday there were infantry exercises. Military attachés from various diplomatic corps were invited to attend. This is the first time since the European War. (Havas, 20th)

Portugal's Diplomatic Policy Develops Strength in the Atlantic, Maintains Friendship with Britain and Brazil 22

Portuguese Capital: Prime Minister Salazar recently issued a lengthy statement reviewing the activities of various government departments. Regarding foreign policy, he stated, "Portugal's traditional policy is to avoid being involved in the vortex of European disputes as much as possible, to maintain friendly relations with Spain, and to develop its strength in the Atlantic Ocean, because Portugal is purely an Atlantic country, and Portugal's colonies are an integral part of its national territory, which is very different from the nature of other countries' colonies. Therefore, its foreign policy must be developed in the Atlantic." Salazar then mentioned Portugal's long-standing friendly relationship with Britain, saying, "The relationship between Portugal and Britain is obviously closely linked, so the authorities of both countries will certainly be able to maintain this friendship and remain unchanged for a long time. We must also strive to promote and enhance the friendly relations between the two countries, but at the same time, Portugal itself must also have some needs, which we have repeatedly mentioned before." (Havas, 20th)

New American Canal Begins Construction, Connecting the Atlantic and the Gulf of Mexico

Hyde Park, New York: The new Florida Canal, connecting the Atlantic and the Gulf of Mexico, held a groundbreaking ceremony today. President Roosevelt pressed an electric bell here, and the first explosives used in Wakulla County exploded. After the new canal is built in the future, it will be the world's largest waterway since the opening of the Panama Canal. (Reuters, 19th)

Spanish Cabinet Resigns En Masse 23

Madrid: Prime Minister Lerroux submitted the entire government's resignation today because the Agrarian Party decided to approve the resignation of two cabinet members belonging to the party. The Lerroux government was formed on October 4 of last year and was the first government to receive majority support in Congress after the general election. (Reuters, 20th)

Madrid: Naval Minister Villalonga resigned on Tuesday, and Agricultural Minister Vallespinosa also resigned yesterday in protest against certain government agencies still being controlled by the Catalan authorities. Vallespinosa was the second member of the Agrarian Party to resign. However, the two agreed to remain responsible pending a resolution of talks between Prime Minister Lerroux, President Zamora, and the leaders of the majority party, so that the austerity plan would be followed in the future. The austerity plan recommends the abolition of three ministers, four vice-ministers, and twenty other official positions. The Minister of Finance reported to the cabinet meeting that the currently implemented austerity plan can save 400 million pesetas, and the continued implementation of the austerity plan will save another 400 million pesetas. (National News Agency, 20th)

Bertrand Russell Disapproves of the Actions of Britain and Italy 24

(Paris) World-renowned political, social, economic, and philosophical scholar Bertrand Russell told Associated Press reporters today that the United States cannot avoid being drawn into the vortex of any war in Europe, and said, "I greatly appreciate the United States' eagerness to seek a policy of neutrality, but when war breaks out, I do not believe that this plan will work. For example, in the last world war, the United States also tried hard to strictly adhere to neutrality, but it was ineffective, because there are economic factors that make it difficult for the United States to stay out of it. What Italy is doing today is indeed stubborn and evil, and what Britain is doing is also stupid. Britain really should not be so strongly opposed to Italy. We must assess the facts and know that Abyssinia is not important if it is viewed from the perspective of Europe and the whole world. If the war spreads, Europe and the whole world will be affected. For the sake of the world, we should try to make things difficult, and if necessary, we should not hesitate to sacrifice Abyssinia." (National News Agency, 19th)

My Request for a Council Seat Declaration Serves as a Warning to the League of Nations

###

So That [The League] Knows My Country Attaches Extraordinary Importance to the Problem, Regret That the Opium Report Did Not Involve the Northeast Opium Disaster

(Geneva) Tonight, the Chinese government's declaration on requesting a seat on the Council of the League of Nations is spreading here and is regarded in League of Nations lounges as a serious warning from the Chinese government to the League of Nations, so that the League of Nations knows that the Chinese government attaches great importance to the issue. (Reuters, 19th)

(Geneva) Today, when the League of Nations General Assembly Committee discussed the opium report, Dr. Hu Shih-tse, the Chinese minister to Switzerland, thanked the reporter for his comments on the Chinese government's efforts to eradicate the opium scourge. He said that the legal production of opium still exceeds the world's legitimate needs, that secret manufacturing has increased, and that private trafficking is even worse than before. Russia has not yet joined the 1931 Convention, and the League of Nations has failed to report on the opium situation in Manchuria and Jehol, which he deeply regrets. Since the manufacturing of narcotics is unrestricted, the world situation will definitely not be satisfactory. (Reuters, 19th)

國際商業電訊

—September 20th Reuters Special Business Telegram—

Gold and Silver

British Gold The London gold price today is 141 shillings and 4 pence, up 4 pence.

British Silver In the London silver market, the spot price today is 29 pence and 31/8ths, and the futures price is 29 pence and 3/8ths, both up 1/8ths. India and China are engaged in both buying and selling, and the market is stable.

Exchange Rates

US-British The London foreign exchange market continued to see demand for US dollars this morning. The opening exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar was $4.921875, which was 31/8ths higher than yesterday's closing rate. After the first hour, it fell by 3/8ths. At 2 pm, it rose by 43/8ths to $4.9225.

British-French The opening price fell by two pounds sterling to 74 francs 76. At noon, it continued to fall by seven pounds sterling. At 2 pm, it rebounded by three pounds sterling to 74 francs 72.

Cotton and Wheat

US Cotton The tense situation in Europe caused the price of cotton in Liverpool to rise again, leading to a rise in the New York cotton market at the opening. Although there was hedging, it could not affect the market price. At the opening, foreign merchants were keen to buy, but later subsided. Then, the impact of hedging began to be felt. At 11 o'clock, it was 8 pence lower than the opening.

British Cotton The Liverpool cotton market also rose. At 1 pm, the October futures price rose by 8 pence to 6.04.

British Wheat The Liverpool wheat market was strong due to the tense situation in Europe. At 1 pm, the October futures price was 6 shillings, 9 pence and 3/8ths, up 1.5 pence.

US Wheat The price of wheat in Liverpool soared, followed by the Chicago wheat market. The opening price rose by 2.5, and miscellaneous grains rose by half a pence. The rise was too rapid, and then gradually fell, and the price dropped. The latest price was 1 pound and 3.5 lower than the opening price.

Rubber

London The London rubber market was stable this morning. At noon, the January and March futures prices were 5 pence 625, unchanged.

New York The New York rubber market opened with a rise of 6 pence. Then, due to good demand, the price continued to rise. The upward trend continued unabated in the morning.

Securities

New York The New York stock market opened this morning with general profit-taking, causing the prices of various stocks to fall. The decline subsided at 10:40 am. After that, prices rebounded slightly, but traders felt uneasy, and the decline resumed. The average price of the Dow Jones 30 industrial stocks opened at 130.75, down 69 pence. 長江秋汛盛漲　鄂境提防復潰

—Hankou Official and Business Jointly Organize Embankment Association— According to a Hankou dispatch, since the floodwaters of the Yangtze River receded, the disaster in Hubei Province had already come to an end. Relief efforts for agriculture and disaster relief had been implemented separately. Unexpectedly, since the beginning of autumn, the upstream water level has risen again. The water level in Zhijiang has risen by more than a Zhang (10 Chinese feet). In various places, some embankments have already been repaired, some are under construction, and some are still being planned. Once the autumn flood returns, all are in extreme danger. On the 19th, the General Headquarters, the Provincial Government, and the General Relief Association received an urgent telegram from Wang Xu, the Magistrate of Songzi County, stating that the Pei Xing, Xi Da, Yongding, Yongbao, and Qi Shuo embankments under the county's jurisdiction had collapsed again, flooding more than 100,000 acres of farmland. At the same time, the Honglin and Li Jia embankments in Jianli were also breached again by the floodwaters. Five locations on the Jin Embankment were leaking, creating an extremely dangerous situation. There are still many unrepaired breaches, and there is a risk of flooding at any time. Although the embankments in Wuhan are relatively solid, preparations must still be made. Currently, an Embankment Research Committee is being jointly organized by officials and businesses, with Huang Wenzhi, Zhou Xingtang, He Hengfu, Xu Weirong, She Baili, Hu Zhichu, Kondo Soji, Bigeer, and Zhao Zhongxuan as members, responsible for planning to raise and thicken the embankments to defend against floods and protect Wuhan. The unrepaired civil embankments in various counties will be repaired by the Disaster Relief Association with the 3 million yuan allocated by the central government. This fund has not yet been allocated, making it impossible to start work. According to previous statistics, the number of disaster victims in various places exceeds 7 million, and it is increasing daily. The cold weather adds another layer of pressure. Under the dual pressures of hunger and cold, it is inevitable that communist bandits will take the opportunity to incite them. Meng Guangpeng, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs and Chairman of the Disaster Relief Association, reported at the second fundraising meeting the other day that slogans issued by bandits such as "Go to Wuhan to get relief" have appeared in areas where disaster victims are gathered. Therefore, the disaster relief issue is of great importance to public security. Recognizing this, Chairman Chiang recently telegraphed the Provincial Government, instructing them to actively engage in relief and comfort for the disaster victims in various places, while also paying attention to changes in the household registration in the disaster areas, and holding the commissioners and magistrates of each county responsible for careful handling.
